ConsumerPerfOptions(args);\n            AtomicLong totalMessagesRead = new AtomicLong(0);\n            AtomicLong totalBytesRead = new AtomicLong(0);\n            AtomicLong joinTimeMs = new   metrics = consumer.metrics();\n            consumer.close();\n\n            // print final stats\n            double elapsedSec = (endMs - startMs) / 1_000.0;\n            long fetchTimeInMs = newFieldsInHeader);\n    }\n\n    private static void consume(KafkaConsumer<byte[], byte[]> consumer,\n                                ConsumerPerfOptions options,\n                                AtomicLong totalMessagesRead,\n                                AtomicLong totalBytesRead,\n                                AtomicLong joinTimeMs,\n                                long bytesRead,\n                                long messagesRead,\n                                long lastBytesRead,\n                                long lastMessagesRead,\n                                long joinStartMs,\n                                AtomicLong joinTimeMsInSingleRound) {\n        long numMessages = options.numMessages();\n        long recordFetchTimeoutMs = options.recordFetchTimeoutMs();\n        long reportingIntervalMs = options.reportingIntervalMs();\n        boolean showDetailedStats = options.showDetailedStats();\n        SimpleDateFormat dateFormat = options.dateFormat();\n        consumer.subscribe(options.topic(),\n            new ConsumerPerfRebListener(joinTimeMs, joinStartMs, joinTimeMsInSingleRound));\n\n        // now start the benchmark\n        long currentTimeMs = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        long lastReportTimeMs = currentTimeMs;\n        long lastConsumedTimeMs = currentTimeMs;\n\n        while (messagesRead < numMessages && currentTimeMs - lastConsumedTimeMs <= recordFetchTimeoutMs) {\n            ConsumerRecords<byte[], byte[]> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n            currentTimeMs = System.currentTimeMillis();\n            if (!records.isEmpty())\n                lastConsumedTimeMs = currentTimeMs;\n            for (ConsumerRecord<byte[], byte[]> record : records) {\n                messagesRead += 1;\n                if (record.key() != null)\n                    bytesRead += record.key().length;\n                if (record.value() != null)\n                    bytesRead += record.value().length;\n                if (currentTimeMs - lastReportTimeMs >= reportingIntervalMs) {\n                    if (showDetailedStats)\n                        printConsumerProgress(0, bytesRead, lastBytesRead, messagesRead, lastMessagesRead,\n                            lastReportTimeMs, currentTimeMs, dateFormat, joinTimeMsInSingleRound.get());\n                    joinTimeMsInSingleRound = new AtomicLong(0);\n                    lastReportTimeMs = currentTimeMs;\n                    lastMessagesRead = messagesRead;\n                    lastBytesRead = bytesRead;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (messagesRead < numMessages)\n            System.out.printf(\"WARNING: Exiting before consuming the expected number of messages: timeout (%d ms) exceeded. \" +\n                \"You can use the --timeout option to increase the timeout.%n\", recordFetchTimeoutMs);\n        totalMessagesRead.set(messagesRead);\n        totalBytesRead.set(bytesRead);\n    }\n\n    protected static void printConsumerProgress(int id,\n                                                long bytesRead,\n                                                long lastBytesRead,\n                                                long messagesRead,\n                                                long lastMessagesRead,\n                                                long startMs,\n                                                long endMs,\n                                                SimpleDateFormat dateFormat,\n messagesRead,\n                                           long lastMessagesRead,\n                                           long startMs,\n                                           long endMs,\n                                           SimpleDateFormat dateFormat) {\n        double elapsedMs = endMs - startMs;\n        double totalMbRead = (bytesRead * 1.0) / (1024 * 1024);\n        double           long messagesRead,\n                                              long lastMessagesRead,\n                                              long startMs,\n intervalMbRead / fetchTimeMs;\n        double intervalMessagesPerSec = (fetchTimeMs <= 0) ? 0.0 : 1000.0 * intervalMessagesRead / fetchTimeMs;\n        System.out.printf(\", %d, %d, %.4f, %.4f\", createFromArgs(ArgumentParser parser, String[] args) throws ArgumentParserException {\n   622→        Namespace res = parser.parseArgs(args);\n   623→\n   624→        boolean useAutoCommit = use slightly different configuration, hence these arguments are conditional.\n   642→        //\n   643→        // See the Python class/method VerifiableConsumer.start_cmd() in verifiable_consumer.py for how the\n   644→        // command line arguments are passed in by the system test framework.\n   645→        if (groupProtocol == GroupProtocol.CONSUMER) {\n   646→            String consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_REMOTE_ASSIGNOR_CONFIG, groupRemoteAssignor);\n   650→        } else {\n   651→            // This means we're using the CLASSIC consumer group protocol.\n   652→            consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG, res.getString(\"assignmentStrategy\"));\n   653→        }\n   654→\n   655→        Integer sessionTimeout = res.getInt(\"sessionTimeout\");\n   656→        if (sessionTimeout != null) {\n   657→            consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.SESSION_TIMEOUT_MS_CONFIG, Integer.toString(sessionTimeout));\n   658→        }\n   659→\n   660→        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_ID_CONFIG, res.getString(\"groupId\"));\n   661→\n   662→        String groupInstanceId = res.getString(\"groupInstanceId\");\n   663→        if (groupInstanceId != null) {\n   664→            consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_INSTANCE_ID_CONFIG, groupInstanceId);\n   665→        }\n   666→\n   667→        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG, brokerHostandPort);\n   668→\n   669→        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG, useAutoCommit);\n   670→        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.AUTO_OFFSET_RESET_CONFIG, res.getString(\"resetPolicy\"));\n   671→\n   672→        StringDeserializer deserializer = new StringDeserializer();\n   673→        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(consumerProps, deserializer, deserializer);\n   674→\n   675→        String topic = 685→                false,\n   686→                verbose);\n   687→    }\n   688→\n   689→    public static void main(String[] args) {\n   690→        ArgumentParser parser = argParser();\n   691→        if (args.length == 0) {\n   692→            parser.printHelp();\n   693→            // Can't use `Exit.exit` here because it didn't exist until 0.11.0.0.\n   694→            System.exit(0);\n static net.sourceforge.argparse4j.impl.Arguments.storeTrue;\n\n/**\n * Command line consumer designed for system testing. It outputs consumer events to STDOUT as JSON\n * formatted objects. The \"name\" field in each JSON event identifies the event type. The following\n * events are currently supported:\n *\n * <ul>\n * <li>partitions_revoked: outputs the partitions revoked through {@link ConsumerRebalanceListener#onPartitionsRevoked(Collection)}.\n *     See {@link org.apache.kafka.tools.VerifiableConsumer.PartitionsRevoked}</li>\n * <li>partitions_assigned: outputs the partitions assigned through {@link ConsumerRebalanceListener#onPartitionsAssigned(Collection)}\n *     See {@link org.apache.kafka.tools.VerifiableConsumer.PartitionsAssigned}.</li>\n * <li>records_consumed: contains a summary of records consumed in a single call to {@link KafkaConsumer#poll(Duration)}.\n *     See {@link org.apache.kafka.tools.VerifiableConsumer.RecordsConsumed}.</li>\n * <li>record_data: contains the key, value, and offset of an individual consumed record (only included if verbose\n *     output is enabled). See {@link org.apache.kafka.tools.VerifiableConsumer.RecordData}.</li>\n * <li>offsets_committed: The result of every offset commit (only included if auto-commit is not enabled).\n *     See {@link org.apache.kafka.tools.VerifiableConsumer.OffsetsCommitted}</li>\n * <li>shutdown_complete: emitted after the consumer returns from {@link KafkaConsumer#close()}.\n *     See {@link org.apache.kafka.tools.VerifiableConsumer.ShutdownComplete}.</li>\n * </ul>\n */\npublic class VerifiableConsumer implements Closeable, OffsetCommitCallback, ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n\n    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(VerifiableConsumer.class);\n\n    private final ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();\n    private final PrintStream out;\n    private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n    private final String topic;\n    private final boolean useAutoCommit;\n    private final boolean useAsyncCommit;\n    private final boolean verbose;\n    private final int maxMessages;\n    private final CountDownLatch shutdownLatch = new CountDownLatch(1);\n    private int consumedMessages = 0;\n\n    public VerifiableConsumer(KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer,\n                              PrintStream out,\n                              String topic,\n                              int maxMessages,\n                              boolean useAutoCommit,\n                              boolean useAsyncCommit,\n                              boolean verbose) {\n        this.consumer = consumer;\n        this.out = out;\n        this.topic = topic;\n        this.maxMessages = maxMessages;\n        this.useAutoCommit = useAutoCommit;\n        this.useAsyncCommit = useAsyncCommit;\n        this.verbose = verbose;\n        addKafkaSerializerModule();\n    }\n\n    private void addKafkaSerializerModule() {\n        SimpleModule kafka = new SimpleModule();\n        kafka.addSerializer(TopicPartition.class, new JsonSerializer<TopicPartition>() {\n            @Override\n            public void serialize(TopicPartition tp, JsonGenerator gen, SerializerProvider serializers) throws IOException {\n                gen.writeStartObject();\n                gen.writeObjectField(\"topic\", tp.topic());\n                gen.writeObjectField(\"partition\", tp.partition());\n                gen.writeEndObject();\n            }\n        });\n        mapper.registerModule(kafka);\n    }\n\n    private boolean hasMessageLimit() {\n        return maxMessages >= 0;\n    }\n\n    private boolean isFinished() {\n        return hasMessageLimit() && consumedMessages >= maxMessages;\n    }\n\n    private Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> onRecordsReceived(ConsumerRecords<String, String> records) {\n        Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = new HashMap<>();\n\n        List<RecordSetSummary> summaries = new ArrayList<>();\n        for (TopicPartition tp : records.partitions()) {\n            List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(tp);\n\n            if (hasMessageLimit() && consumedMessages + partitionRecords.size() > maxMessages)\n                partitionRecords = partitionRecords.subList(0, maxMessages - consumedMessages);\n\n            if (partitionRecords.isEmpty())\n                continue;\n\n            long minOffset = partitionRecords.get(0).offset();\n            long maxOffset = partitionRecords.get(partitionRecords.size() - 1).offset();\n\n            offsets.put(tp, new OffsetAndMetadata(maxOffset + 1));\n            summaries.add(new RecordSetSummary(tp.topic(), tp.partition(),\n                    partitionRecords.size(), minOffset, maxOffset));\n\n            if (verbose) {\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : partitionRecords) {\n                    printJson(new RecordData(record));\n                }\n            }\n\n            consumedMessages += partitionRecords.size();\n            if (isFinished())\n                break;\n        }\n\n        printJson(new RecordsConsumed(records.count(), summaries));\n        return offsets;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onComplete(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Exception exception) {\n        List<CommitData> committedOffsets = new ArrayList<>();\n        for (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsetEntry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n            TopicPartition tp = offsetEntry.getKey();\n            committedOffsets.add(new CommitData(tp.topic(), tp.partition(), offsetEntry.getValue().offset()));\n        }\n\n        boolean success = true;\n        String error = null;\n        if (exception != null) {\n            success = false;\n            error = exception.getMessage();\n        }\n        printJson(new OffsetsCommitted(committedOffsets, error, success));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        printJson(new PartitionsAssigned(partitions));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        printJson(new PartitionsRevoked(partitions));\n    }\n\n    private void printJson(Object data) {\n        try {\n            out.println(mapper.writeValueAsString(data));\n        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {\n            out.println(\"Bad data can't be written as json: \" + e.getMessage());\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets) {\n        try {\n            consumer.commitSync(offsets);\n            onComplete(offsets, null);\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            // we only call wakeup() once to close the consumer, so this recursion should be safe\n            commitSync(offsets);\n            throw e;\n        } catch (FencedInstanceIdException e) {\n            throw e;\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            onComplete(offsets, e);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void run() {\n        try {\n            printJson(new StartupComplete());\n            consumer.subscribe(Collections.singletonList(topic), this);\n\n            while (!isFinished()) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(Long.MAX_VALUE));\n                Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = onRecordsReceived(records);\n\n                if (!useAutoCommit) {\n                    if (useAsyncCommit)\n                        consumer.commitAsync(offsets, this);\n                    else\n                        commitSync(offsets);\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            // ignore, we are closing\n            log.trace(\"Caught WakeupException because consumer is shutdown, ignore and terminate.\", e);\n        } catch (Throwable t) {\n            // Log the error so it goes to the service log and not stdout\n            log.error(\"Error during processing, terminating consumer process: \", t);\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n            printJson(new ShutdownComplete());\n            shutdownLatch.countDown();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void close() {\n        boolean interrupted = false;\n        try {\n            consumer.wakeup();\n            while (true) {\n                try {\n                    shutdownLatch.await();\n                    return;\n                } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n                    interrupted = true;\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            if (interrupted)\n                Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n        }\n    }\n\n    @JsonPropertyOrder({ \"timestamp\", \"name\" })\n    private abstract static class ConsumerEvent {\n        private final long timestamp = System.currentTimeMillis();\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public abstract String name();\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public long timestamp() {\n            return timestamp;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class StartupComplete extends ConsumerEvent {\n\n        @Override\n        public String name() {\n            return \"startup_complete\";\n        }\n    }\n\n    private public String name() {\n            return \"partitions_revoked\";\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class PartitionsAssigned extends ConsumerEvent {\n        private final Collection<TopicPartition> partitions;\n\n        public PartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n            this.partitions = partitions;\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public Collection<TopicPartition> partitions() {\n            return partitions;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public String name() {\n            return \"partitions_assigned\";\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static class RecordsConsumed extends ConsumerEvent {\n        private final long count;\n        private final List<RecordSetSummary> partitionSummaries;\n\n        public RecordsConsumed(long count, List<RecordSetSummary> partitionSummaries) {\n            this.count = count;\n            this.partitionSummaries = partitionSummaries;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public String name() {\n            return \"records_consumed\";\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public long count() {\n            return count;\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public List<RecordSetSummary> partitions() {\n            return partitionSummaries;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @JsonPropertyOrder({ \"timestamp\", \"name\", \"key\", \"value\", \"topic\", \"partition\", \"offset\" })\n    public static class RecordData extends ConsumerEvent {\n\n        private final ConsumerRecord<String, String> record;\n\n        public }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public String topic() {\n            return record.topic();\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public int partition() {\n            return   return record.value();\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public long offset() {\n            return record.offset();\n        }\n\n    }\n\n    private static class PartitionData {\n        private final String topic;\n        private final int partition;\n\n        public PartitionData(String topic, int partition) {\n            this.topic = topic;\n            this.partition = partition;\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public String topic() {\n            return topic;\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public int partition() {\n            return        this.success = success;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public String name() {\n            return \"offsets_committed\";\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public private final long offset;\n\n        public CommitData(String topic, int partition, long offset) {\n            super(topic, partition);\n            this.offset = offset;\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public long offset() {\n            return offset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class RecordSetSummary extends PartitionData {\n        private final long count;\n        private final long minOffset;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n\n        public RecordSetSummary(String topic, int partition, long count, long minOffset, long maxOffset) {\n            super(topic, partition);\n            this.count = count;\n            this.minOffset = minOffset;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        @JsonProperty\n        public long .newArgumentParser(\"verifiable-consumer\")\n                .defaultHelp(true)\n                .description(\"This tool consumes messages from a specific topic and emits consumer events (e.g. group rebalances, received messages, and offsets committed) as JSON objects to STDOUT.\");\n        MutuallyExclusiveGroup connectionGroup = parser.addMutuallyExclusiveGroup(\"Connection Group\")\n                .description(\"Group of arguments for connection to brokers\")\n                .required(true);\n        connectionGroup.addArgument(\"--bootstrap-server\")\n                .action(store())\n                .required(true)\n                .type(String.class)\n                .metavar(\"HOST1:PORT1[,HOST2:PORT2[...]]\")\n                .dest(\"bootstrapServer\")\n                .help(\"The server(s) to connect to.      .type(String.class)\n                .metavar(\"CONFIG_FILE\")\n                .help(\"Consumer config properties file (config options shared with command line parameters will be overridden).\");\n\n        return parser;\n    }\n\n    public static VerifiableConsumer createFromArgs(ArgumentParser parser, String[] args) throws ArgumentParserException {\n        Namespace res = parser.parseArgs(args);\n\n        boolean useAutoCommit = res.getBoolean(\"useAutoCommit\");\n        String configFile = res.getString(\"consumer.config\");\n        String brokerHostandPort = res.getString(\"bootstrapServer\");\n\n        Properties consumerProps = new Properties();\n        if (configFile != null) {\n            try {\n                consumerProps.putAll(Utils.loadProps(configFile));\n            } catch (IOException e) {\n                throw new ArgumentParserException(e.getMessage(), parser);\n            }\n        }\n\n        GroupProtocol groupProtocol = GroupProtocol.of(res.getString(\"groupProtocol\"));\n        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_PROTOCOL_CONFIG, groupProtocol.name());\n\n        // 3.7.0 includes support for KIP-848 which introduced a new implementation of the consumer group protocol.\n        // The two implementations use slightly different configuration, hence these arguments are conditional.\n        //\n        // See the Python class/method VerifiableConsumer.start_cmd() in verifiable_consumer.py for how the\n        // command line arguments are passed in by the system test framework.\n        if (groupProtocol == GroupProtocol.CONSUMER) {\n            String groupRemoteAssignor = res.getString(\"groupRemoteAssignor\");\n\n            if (groupRemoteAssignor != null)\n                consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_REMOTE_ASSIGNOR_CONFIG, groupRemoteAssignor);\n        } else {\n            // This means we're using the CLASSIC consumer group protocol.\n            consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG, res.getString(\"assignmentStrategy\"));\n        }\n\n        Integer sessionTimeout = res.getInt(\"sessionTimeout\");\n        if (sessionTimeout != null) {\n            consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.SESSION_TIMEOUT_MS_CONFIG, Integer.toString(sessionTimeout));\n        }\n\n        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_ID_CONFIG, res.getString(\"groupId\"));\n\n        String groupInstanceId = res.getString(\"groupInstanceId\");\n        if (groupInstanceId != null) {\n            consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_INSTANCE_ID_CONFIG, groupInstanceId);\n        }\n\n        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG, brokerHostandPort);\n\n        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG, useAutoCommit);\n        consumerProps.put(ConsumerConfig.AUTO_OFFSET_RESET_CONFIG, res.getString(\"resetPolicy\"));\n\n        StringDeserializer deserializer = new StringDeserializer();\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(consumerProps, deserializer, deserializer);\n\n        String topic = res.getString(\"topic\");\n        int maxMessages = res.getInt(\"maxMessages\");\n        boolean verbose = res.getBoolean(\"verbose\");\n\n        return new VerifiableConsumer(\n                consumer,\n                System.out,\n                topic,\n                maxMessages,\n                useAutoCommit,\n                false,\n                verbose);\n    }\n\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        ArgumentParser parser = argParser();\n        if (args.length == 0) {\n            parser.printHelp();\n            // Can't use `Exit.exit` here because it didn't exist until 0.11.0.0.\n            System.exit(0);\n        }\n        try {\n            final VerifiableConsumer consumer = createFromArgs(parser, args);\n            // Can't use InventoryConsumer(String bootstrapServers, String groupId) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG, bootstrapServers);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_ID_CONFIG, groupId);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.KEY_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.VALUE_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.AUTO_OFFSET_RESET_CONFIG, \"earliest\");\n }\n\n                // Commit offsets after processing batch\n                consumer.commitSync();\n            }\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            LOG.info(\"Consumer shutdown duplicate messages gracefully\n            // This ensures that processing the same message multiple times produces the same result\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            LOG.error(\"Error
